the turningpoint OF the middl age

If pontif innoc  papal power
attain greatest height yet one predecessor
chair st peter becam throne almost absolut supremaci thi
mighti pontiff gregori whose real name hildebrand indic
german descent born son carpent tuscani
He becam monk benedictin order educ
abbey cluni franc In went rome call papal
elect saw abus moment fix mind
upon strive abolish In rome soon rose
rank cardin

for mani year hildebrand real director papal polici
long elect pope work accomplish
reform distinguish pontif continu till
death

As part holi roman empir itali held dual relat
emperor pope between roman pontiff secular head
empir struggl supremaci long often bitter
At time hildebrand activ appear papaci state
degrad demor church

long elev papal chair hildebrand effort
met much success power holi see gradual
increas independ emperor whose hitherto
govern papal elect chiefli influenc
hildebrand pope nichola chosen new method
